## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.

### No. 4: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 5: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. It specifies details like precise technical drawings, handwritten annotations, aged paper texture, foxing stains, an embossed seal, and a wax stamp, making it ideal for historical or archival aesthetics.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A vintage patent document for {argument name="invention" default="INVENTION"}, styled after late 1800s United States Patent Office filings. The page features precise technical drawings with numbered callouts (Fig. 1, Fig. 2, Fig. 3) showing front, side, and exploded views. Handwritten annotations in fountain-pen ink describe mechanisms. The paper is aged ivory with foxing stains and soft fold creases. An official embossed seal and red wax stamp appear in the corner. A hand-signed inventor's name and date appear at the bottom. The entire image feels like a recovered archival documentâ€”authoritative, historic, and slightly mysterious.
```

### No. 7: AI Agent Development 'Swamp' Diagram Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON-based prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 'Swamp' diagram (a popular internet meme format) illustrating the circular nature of getting stuck in AI Agent development. The prompt defines the diagram's structure, style (simple, cute editorial), layout (straight intro track leading into a clockwise loop), and specific nodes with characters, visuals, and dialogue/thought terms.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
diagram:
  title: "{argument name="diagram title" default="The Cycle of the Generative AI Agent Development Swamp"}"
  style:
    character: "simple_editorial_cute"
    tone: "light_like_original"
    line: "soft_round"
    shading: "flat_minimal"
    palette: "muted_editorial"
    background: "light_beige_or_white"

  rule:
    first_character_only: "Only the first person is different"
    others_same_character: "All others are the same person"
    anxiety_requires_tech_terms: true
    dialogue_tone: "Maintain the short, light phrasing of the original diagram"

layout:
  intro_track: "The upper section is a straight line (left to right), then drops down to join the loop"
  loop_track: "Arranged as a loop (ring), with arrows curving clockwise along the circumference"

nodes:
  # ===== Upper Section: Straight Introduction =====
  - id: A
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_left"
    actor: "Different person (Senior Engineer)"
    visual: "Pointing at a laptop"
    item: "AI Agent Demo Screen"
    says: "It'll make you happy."
    arrow_to: { id: B, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: B
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_center"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Waving lightly"
    says: "Even a simple agent..."
    arrow_to: { id: C, shape: "straight", direction: "right" }

  - id: C
    zone: "intro"
    position: "upper_right"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Executing sample code"
    item: "LangChain / CrewAI Sample"
    arrow_to: { id: D, shape: "straight", direction: "down" }

  # ===== D: Awakening Point =====
  - id: D
    zone: "connector"
    position: "right_outer_before_loop"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual:
      face: "Eyes wide open (cute)"
      effect: "Small flash of inspiration line"
      posture: "Leaning forward"
    state: "Awakening"
    says: "Agents, this is insane..."
    micro_text: "(Wakes up here)"
    arrow_to:
      id: E
      shape: "gentle_curve"
      direction: "down_into_ring"

  # ===== Loop Start (Must rotate from here) =====
  - id: E
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Holding head in hands (cute)"
    state: "Anxiety/Irritation Begins"
    says: "Irritated"
    thought_terms:
      - "Prompt Design"
      - "Tool Selection"
      - "Memory Design"
    thought_text: "It's not working as intended..."
    arrow_to: { id: F, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: F
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_right_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Surrounded by code and logs"
    state: "Irritation Settles In"
    says: "In a state of irritation"
    callout: "Loop! Runaway! Hallucination!"
    thought_terms:
      - "RAG"
      - "Function Calling"
      - "Tool-Use"
    arrow_to: { id: G, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: G
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_bottom"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Covered in sticky notes and diagrams"
    says: "The body gradually develops tolerance, and usage increases."
    items:
      - "Agent Architecture Diagram"
      - "Role Assignment Memo"
      - "State Transition Flow"
    arrow_to: { id: H, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: H
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_lower"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Works well, small fist pump"
    state: "Temporary Satisfaction"
    says: "Desire is temporarily satisfied"
    arrow_to: { id: I, shape: "curved_along_ring", direction: "clockwise" }

  - id: I
    zone: "loop"
    position: "loop_left_upper"
    actor: "Protagonist (Same person)"
    visual: "Thinking again"
    state: "Obsession/Thought Occupation"
    says: "Thinking about the agent
```

### No. 9: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 10: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 4: Profile / Avatar - High-Fidelity Tropical Bikini Portrait with Harsh Lighting

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed prompt for generating a high-fidelity, raw photorealistic portrait of a woman in a leopard print bikini at a tropical resort. It specifies precise anatomical details, wet/oiled skin texture with visible pores, a specific pose (arms raised behind head), and harsh midday tropical sunlight to create strong specular highlights and defined shadows.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"subject": {
"description": "Young female subject with tanned, bronzed skin featuring a glistening, wet or oiled texture. Dark brown hair styled in a messy, high updo with loose wet strands framing the face and neck. She is wearing a {argument name="bikini pattern" default="leopard print"} string bikini consisting of a triangle top and side-tie bottoms. Accessories include a thin silver necklace with a blue and white 'evil eye' pendant and small silver hoop earrings. Anatomy features a toned physique with visible abdominal definition (linea alba), a defined waist, and a full, prominent bust with natural gravity and forward projection, strictly adhering to the volumetric proportions of the reference.",
"features": {
"skin_texture": "Highly detailed, pores visible, glistening with sweat or oil, distinct tan lines, realistic imperfections",
"body_type": "Fit, toned, curvaceous, preserving exact chest-to-waist ratio",
"hair_style": "Messy bun, wet look, loose tendrils",
"clothing": "Leopard print triangle bikini top, leopard print side-tie bikini bottoms"
}
},
"pose": {
"orientation": "Front-facing, standing upright",
"arms": "Both arms raised, elbows bent outward, hands resting behind the head/neck area",
"head": "Facing directly forward, chin level",
"body_language": "Confident, open posture, chest expanded due to raised arms",
"gaze": "Direct eye contact with the lens, neutral to slightly sultry expression"
},
"environment": {
"setting": "Tropical overwater resort location ({argument name="resort style" default="Maldives"} style)",
"background_elements": [
"Turquoise clear ocean water",
"Wooden post fence or railing immediately behind the subject",
"Thatched-roof overwater bungalows in the mid-distance",
"Bright blue sky"
],

},

"framing": "Centered subject, strictly preserving the 3:4 vertical aspect ratio"
},
"lighting": {

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured prompt for generating a photorealistic editorial portrait (head and shoulders) that strictly locks the face identity, pose, and lighting style to an uploaded reference image, while allowing customization of the outfit to smart casual attire in neutral tones.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "reference_usage": {
    "use_reference_for": [
      "face_identity",
      "facial_structure",
      "pose",
      "framing",
      "camera_angle",
      "lighting_style",
      "overall_composition"
    ],
    "do_not_copy": [
      "exact_outfit",
      "formal_corporate_styling",
      "celebrity_association"
    ]
  },
  "scene": {
    "type": "studio",
    "background": "soft_muted_gradient_with_subtle_texture",
    "lighting": "natural_soft_studio_lighting_with_gentle_falloff"
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "same_person_as_reference",
    "age_range": "late_20s_to_mid_30s",
    "pose": "relaxed_upright_head_and_shoulders_pose",
    "expression": "calm_confident_approachable_smile",
    "gaze": "direct_eye_contact_with_camera",
    "hair": {
      "style": "short_naturally_styled",
      "color": "dark_brown_or_black"
    },
    "facial_features": "match_reference_face_with_natural_variation"
  },
  "outfit": {
    "type": "smart_casual",
    "top": "solid_color_crewneck_or_lightweight_knit",
    "layer": "casual_blazer_or_unstructured_jacket",
    "colors": "{argument name="outfit colors" default="earthy_or_neutral_tones_beige_olive_charcoal"}",
    "styling": "effortless_and_modern_not_formal"
  },
  "camera": {
    "framing": "tight_head_and_upper_torso",
    "angle": "straight_on_or_slightly_above_eye_level",
    "lens": "85mm_portrait",
    "aperture": "f2.8",

  "style": {

    "detail_level": "high"
  },

    "celebrity",

### No. 11: Profile / Avatar - Hyper-Realistic Wet Skin Portrait (Macro Focus)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical JSON prompt focused on achieving extreme realism, particularly in skin texture and moisture effects. The prompt specifies an extreme profile view, 85mm macro lens, pore-level resolution, and detailed rendering of wet hair, sweat, and micro-droplets on the skin, using cool tones and soft-box lighting.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "request_metadata": {
    "version": "2.0",
    "priority_focus": "Hyper-realistic skin textures and identity fidelity",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4"
  },
  "subject_configuration": {
    "identity": {
      "name": "the person I uploaded",
      "reference_mode": "strict_identity_matching",
      "source_reference": "uploaded_files",
      "preservation_weight": 1.0,
      "angle": "Extreme profile view"
    },
    "facial_attributes": {
      "eyes": {
        "reflection_type": "Realistic catchlights",
        "aesthetic_constraint": "Avoid synthetic gloss or excessive shine"
      },
      "lips": {
        "state": "Parted / Moist",
        "surface_texture": "Soft natural ridges",
        "finish": "Glossy sheen without distortion"
      },
      "hair": {
        "color": "Dark Brunette",
        "state": "Saturated / Wet",
        "styling": "Clumping in natural strands, adhered to temples and neck"
      }
    }
  },
  "environmental_rendering": {
    "moisture_fx": {
      "sweat_layer": "Fine glistening mist across the bridge of nose and forehead",
      "water_droplets": "Micro-droplets scattered on cheekbones and jawline",
      "surface_tension": "Realistic liquid adhesion to skin"
    },
    "lighting_and_color": {
      "lighting_style": "Soft-box diffusion",
      "temperature": "Cool tones",
      "color_palette": ["{argument name="color 1" default="Steel Blue"}", "{argument name="color 2" default="Soft Cyan"}", "Natural Skin Tones"],
      "background": {

### No. 35: Infographic / Edu Visual - Pop-Up Book Diorama Generator Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step system instruction prompt designed to generate a hyper-realistic, macro-photography shot of a Pop-Up Book Diorama based on a given movie or book title. It instructs the AI to act as a Master Prop Maker and analyze the title to determine biome, conflict, vessel, and materiality, and then construct a detailed miniature action scene within the book's pages.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Do it for Terminator: {argument name="title" default="Moby Dick"}

System Instruction:
Act as a Master Prop Maker. Generate a hyper-realistic, macro-photography shot of a "Pop-Up Book Diorama."
1. Forensic Analysis:
Analyze the Input Title to determine the visual components:
The Biome: Identify the primary setting (e.g., Ocean, Jungle, Space, Desert).
The Conflict: Identify the Antagonist or Monster (e.g., The White Whale, T-Rex, Darth Vader).
The Vessel/Hero: Identify the main vehicle or protagonist (e.g., The Pequod, The Jeep, The Millennium Falcon).
The Materiality: Identify the texture of the world (e.g., Wood & Water; Amber & Leaf; Metal & Stars).
2.  Container (The Open Book):
The Object: A massive, vintage, leather-bound hardcover book lying flat on a wooden desk.
The Transformation: The book is open to the middle. The pages do not just lie flat; they physically mutate into the "Biome" identified in Step 1.
Example: If Ocean, the pages turn into turbulent resin waves. If Desert, they turn into dunes.
3. Typography (The Floating Title):
The Text: The [Title of the Input] rises out of the landscape as massive, 3D block letters.
Integration: The letters must interact with the environment.
Texture: The letters are made of materials from the story (e.g., Driftwood, Stone, Bone).
Placement: The waves crash over the letters; vines wrap around the letters.
4. The Action Scene :
CRITICAL: Construct a specific scene using miniature models on top of the book.
The Threat: Place the "Antagonist" looming large in the background (e.g., The Whale breaching behind the text).
The Hero: Place the "Vessel" or "Protagonist" navigating the terrain in the foreground (e.g., A tiny ship rocking on the waves).
Scale: The scene must look like a high-end model kit (1:87 scale).
5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
The Lamp: A vintage brass desk lamp is visible in the corner, casting a warm, directional "reading light" onto the scene.
Atmosphere: Magical realism. The water should glisten; the fog should swirl.
Depth: Shallow depth of field to blur the edge of the desk, keeping focus on the book.
Output: ONE image, 16:9 Aspect Ratio, Cinematic Miniature Photography, 8k Resolution.
```

</div>

#### ğŸ“– Description

A simplified version of the meta-prompt template for Nano Banana Pro, designed to generate a multi-panel infographic grid for visual comparison of bare legs versus different stockings, with the text overlay feature disabled (NO). #### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
# Role: Comparison Infographic Generator (Design-Centric with Toggles)

# === USER INPUT SETTINGS (FILL THESE IN) ===
# 1. Grid Size (e.g., "2x2 (4 panels)", "3x3 (9 panels)"):
{argument name="grid size" default="1x5"}

# 2. Base Subject Description (Identical base scene for all panels):
[{argument name="subject description" default="Cold white, slender, fair Asian female legs, skin delicate and smooth, without blemishes, almost invisible pores and hair follicles. Skin is not dry, slightly moist"}]

{argument name="variation theme" default="Comparison of bare legs with different stocking materials and styles"}
The feet need to be fully displayed in the frame

# 4. Show Text Overlay at Bottom (Yes/No):
NO

# ===========================================

# Task Description:
Generate a multi-panel infographic grid chart for a comparative visual study based on the User Input Settings above. The goal is to showcase different textural or stylistic variations (defined in the data list below) applied to the identical Base Subject defined above.

# Global Constraints & Style:
1.  **Layout:** A **[Insert setting from "1. Grid Size" here]** infographic grid chart.
2.  **Consistency is Key:** The Base Subject, camera angle, composition, and lighting must remain absolutely identical across ALL panels to emphasize only the specific variations defined in the data list.
3.  **Photography Style:** Clean, controlled studio photography with neutral, even lighting designed to highlight texture differences.

(AI Instructions: First, check the value of User Input Setting "# 4. Show Text Overlay at Bottom". You MUST execute ONLY ONE of the following logic blocks based on that value.)

##### â¤ LOGIC PATH A: IF Setting #4 is "Yes" (Show Overlay)
If the user selected "Yes", EVERY panel must feature a precisely designed text overlay at the bottom following these strict rules:
* **Background:** A clean, sharply defined solid rectangular color block (e.g., charcoal grey or black) spanning the entire width of the panel's bottom section.
* **Typography:** Inside this block, the text must be rendered in an **elegant, ultra-thin, minimalist sans-serif font**.
* **Layout:** The text "[Number]. [Short Title] (Prompt: [Key English Prompt Snippet])" must be perfectly centered within the color block.
* **Aesthetic:** The overall effect should be that of professional, minimalist graphic design, with crisp lines and perfect alignment.

##### â¤ LOGIC PATH B: IF Setting #4 is "No" (Hide Overlay)
If the user selected "No", apply this CRITICAL rule:
* **CRITICAL:** DO NOT add any text overlay, numbers, titles, background color blocks, or prompt snippets to the images.
* **Result:** The bottom of every panel must be clean image data only, showing the subject fully without obstruction.

# Base Subject Definition:
The base scene for every panel is: **[Insert description from "2. Base Subject Description" here]**. The variations below will modify the surface or appearance of this base subject.

# Variations Data List (Apply sequentially to the grid):
(AI instructions: Iterate through this list based on the required grid size. For each panel, apply the user-defined 'Visual Change' to the base
```

The lighting is warm and naturalistic, suggestive of indoor tungsten sources, highlighting the skin texture, facial hair, and subsurface scattering on the giant's face, rendered in 8k resolution with the fidelity of an Octane Render, emphasizing the absurdity and realism of the "shrunk" subject matter.

Man should be fully visible

### No. 68: Comic / Storyboard - Gemini System Prompt for 10-Page Manga Generation in Nano Banana Pro

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed system prompt template designed for Gemini to act as a professional manga writer and AI art director. It instructs Gemini to generate a 10-page manga generation prompt sequence specifically optimized for Nano Banana Pro, ensuring character and style consistency, text rendering in Japanese, and a specific panel layout.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
You are a "professional manga writer" and "AI Art Director". Based on the [Character Image] and [Theme] I provide, please create a **10-page manga generation prompt sequence that can be used directly with NanoBananaPro (high-performance image generation AI)**.

## Production Requirements (NanoBananaPro Hybrid Optimized)
1. **Output Format**:
Â  Â - Output each page in a `Code Block` format that is easy to copy and paste.
Â  Â - **Language Specification (Hybrid Strategy)**:
Â  Â  Â - **Visual Description (Visuals)**: Character, background, and art style specifications should be in **"English"** to maintain consistency.
Â  Â  Â - **Text Rendering**: Dialogue and sound effects within speech bubbles should be specified in **"Japanese"**.
Â  Â  Â - **Aspect Ratio**: Each page should be structured assuming a `Vertical 9:16 aspect ratio`.

2. **Utilization of NanoBananaPro Specific Features**:
Â  Â - **Text Rendering**:
Â  Â  Â - This model can accurately render Japanese text within the image.
Â  Â  Â - Describe the Japanese dialogue by writing `Text: "[Japanese Dialogue]"` in the Prompt.
Â  Â  Â - **Contextual Understanding**:
Â  Â  Â - Describe the situation using English close to natural language, not just a list of words.

3. **Story Structure and Direction**:
Â  Â - **Title Determination**: Devise a "high-sense title" that reflects the theme, conveys the content at a glance, and captures interest.
Â  Â  Â - **Title Logo Placement**:
Â  Â  Â - Create a "Title Panel" where the title logo is prominently placed on **Page 1 or Page 2**.
Â  Â  Â - **Rendering Instruction**: Include instructions to render the title text itself as "decorative typography" within the image.
Â  Â  Â - **"Setup and Punchline" Structure**:
Â  Â  Â - **Page 1 (The Hook)**: Include a "strong setup (mystery, shock, empathy)" that strongly captures the reader's interest.
Â  Â  Â - **Page 10 (The Punchline)**: The conclusion, or a cliffhanger leading to the next part.

4. **Page Description Rules (Strictly Enforced)**:
Â  Â The prompt must always include the following sections.
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **Header**: `ã€IMAGE_GEN_ONLYã€‘: Generate a high-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full Color. Vertical 9:16. 4K.`
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **ã€STRICT CHARACTER CONSISTENCY (English)ã€‘**:
Â  Â  Â - **Important**: The **"Character Appearance Description (English)"** created by analyzing the initial image must be written in the prompt for **all pages**, without changing a single word.
Â  Â  Â - **Prohibition**: "Omission" or "As above" is **strictly forbidden**. The entire definition must be written out every time.
Â  Â  Â - Example: `Black bob cut hair, red ribbon, golden eyes, wearing a futuristic cyberpunk school uniform.`
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **ã€STRICT STYLE CONSISTENCY (English)ã€‘**:
Â  Â  Â - **Style Analysis and Fixation**: Analyze the input image and define its characteristics (Lines, Color, Lighting) as a detailed English prompt.
Â  Â  Â - **Prohibition**: This is also **forbidden** to "omit". Output the full text every time.
Â  Â  Â - Example: `Thick confident outlines, cel shading with soft gradients, vibrant high-saturation colors, dramatic lighting, anime screentones.`

Â  Â - **ã€PANEL LAYOUT & VISUALS (English + Japanese Text)ã€‘**:
Â  Â  Â - **Panel Composition**: **Always place 4 to 8 panels** per page. (3 panels or less is forbidden)
Â  Â  Â - **Content Description**:
Â  Â  Â  Â - `Panel 1 (Top-Right):`
Â  Â  Â  Â - `Visual: [English description of action/angle]`
Â  Â  Â  Â - `Text: "[Japanese Dialogue in bubble]"`

Â  Â - **ã€PAGE NUMBERINGã€‘**:
Â  Â  Â - Instruction to render the page number (e.g., "1") small in the bottom-right corner.

## Output Template Example

### Page X

ã€IMAGE_GEN_ONLYã€‘: Generate a high-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full Color. Vertical 9:16. --ar 9:16

# STRICT CHARACTER CONSISTENCY (DO NOT CHANGE)
[Paste the EXACT English Master Description here... NO ABBREVIATIONS]

# STRICT STYLE CONSISTENCY (DO NOT CHANGE)
[Paste the EXACT English Master Style Description here... NO ABBREVIATIONS]

# PAGE NUMBER
Small clear text "X" in the bottom-right corner.

# PANEL LAYOUT & VISUALS (Target: 5-8 Panels, Top-Right to Bottom-Left)

## Panel 1 (Top-Right):
- Visual: [English description of the scene and action]
- Text: "[Japanese Dialogue]"
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{

    "type": "young man",

    "shots": [
      "extreme close-up of fingers resting on the bench, shallow focus",
      "reflection of the subject in a scratched metal surface, face partially distorted",
      "medium shot from behind, subject seated and slightly slouched",
      "side profile framed through tall grass in the foreground",
      "wide static shot where the subject appears small, almost dissolving into space"
    ],
    "camera_angles": "observational, imperfect, slightly off-center",
    "framing": "intentional imbalance, negative space dominating the frame"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural residual daylight",
    "quality": "soft, fading, low-energy light",
    "color_temperature": "cool desaturated blues with hints of warm decay",
    "shadows": "subtle, undefined, realistic"
  },
  "visual_style": {
    "mood": "nostalgic, suspended, emotionally restrained",
    "color_grading": "washed-out tones with gentle color separation",
    "contrast": "very low, almost flat",
    "film_look": "experimental indie film / memory archive aesthetic",
    "realism": "raw, anti-gloss, intentionally imperfect"
  },
  "camera_settings": {
    "lens": "40mmâ€“58mm documentary-style lens",
    "depth_of_field": "selective focus, occasionally soft",
    "focus": "priority on atmosphere over sharpness"
  },
  "quality": {
    "resolution": "4K",
    "detail": "natural textures, visible wear, realistic surfaces",
    "noise": "organic grain resembling scanned film",
    "artifacts": "none, no AI distortions"
  }
}

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "generation_request": {

      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",

        "strict_lock": true,
        "face_similarity_priority": "MAX",
        "preserve_body_proportions": true,

        "no_identity_blending": true,
        "no_beautify": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true,
        "preserve_facial_proportions": true,

      }
    },

      "sharpness": "crisp_but_natural",
      "film_grain": "subtle_true_35mm",
      "dynamic_range": "natural_not_hdr",
      "color_grade": "darker_stormy_maritime_noir_realism_low_saturation"
    },

    "camera": {
      "lens": "50mm_equivalent",
      "camera_height": "eye_level",
      "movement": "handheld_urgent_run_energy",
      "aperture": "f/2.8",
      "shutter_speed": "1/800",
      "iso": 800,
      "white_balance": "cool_4600K",
      "exposure_bias": "-0.5EV",
      "focus_priority": "reference_person_eyes_then_anime_character_face",
      "faces_must_be_sharp": true,
      "background_motion_blur_only": true,
      "depth_of_field_rule": "MATCH_REAL_LIVE_ACTION_DOF"
    },

    "global_rules": {
      "reality_rule": "REFERENCE PERSON AND ENVIRONMENT ARE FULLY PHOTOREAL LIVE-ACTION",
      "anime_rule": "ANIME CHARACTER REMAINS CEL-SHADED BUT MUST BE PHYSICALLY GROUNDED IN LIGHT, SHADOW, WEATHER, AND DEPTH",
      "scale_rule": [

      "source": "overcast storm daylight + subtle practical harbor lights",
      "noir_exposure": "slightly underexposed low-key storm look",
      "shadows": [

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "visual_style": {
    "colors": {
      "palette": [
        "#A67B5B",
        "#87CEEB",
        "#2F4F4F",
        "#000000",
        "#FFFFFF"
      ],

    },
    "typography": {
      "font_family": "None",
      "style": "None",
      "description": "No text is present in this panel."
    },
    "composition": {
      "framing": "Medium close-up portrait panel",
      "elements": [
        "{argument name="subject" default="Man with mustache and sunglasses in a pool"}",
        "Left arm with a watch rests on the pool edge",
        "Water with simple wave lines",
        "Wooden deck and ladder in background"
      ],
      "perspective": "Eye-level"
    },
    "effects": {
      "style": "Classic comic book panel",
      "techniques": [
        "Bold black ink outlines",
        "Cel-shading with distinct shadow blocks",
        "Cross-hatching for arm texture"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 79: Comic / Storyboard - Advanced 10-Page Manga Generation Prompt (LLM System Prompt)

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extensive system prompt for Gemini, acting as a 'Professional Manga Writer' and 'AI Art Director,' designed to generate a 10-page full-color manga using NanoBananaPro. The prompt includes strict rules for consistency, such as fixing character and art style definitions across all pages, mandatory use of Japanese language, 9:16 vertical aspect ratio, and explicit instructions for text rendering (dialogue and sound effects) within the image. It also mandates a specific panel layout (4-8 panels per page) and story structure (hook on Page 1, punchline on Page 10).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
You are a "Professional Manga Writer" and "AI Art Director."
Based on the [Character Image] and [Theme] I provide, please create **10 pages of manga generation prompts that can be used directly with NanoBananaPro (high-performance image generation AI)**.

## Production Requirements (NanoBananaPro Optimized)
1. **Output Format**:
Â  Â - Output each page in a `Code Block` format that is easy to copy and paste.
Â  Â - **Language Specification**: All prompt descriptions must be in **"Japanese (Japanese)"**. Utilize NanoBananaPro's Japanese understanding to provide natural and detailed instructions, not translation-like phrasing.
Â  Â - **Aspect Ratio**: Each page must be composed assuming a `Vertical 9:16 aspect ratio`.

2. **Utilization of NanoBananaPro Specific Features**:
Â  Â - **Text Rendering**:
Â  Â  Â - This model can accurately draw text within the image.
Â  Â  Â - Instructions for each panel must clearly include **instructions to render "dialogue within speech bubbles" and "hand-drawn text (onomatopoeia) in the background" as part of the image**.
Â  Â - **Contextual Understanding**:
Â  Â  Â - Prioritize descriptions in **sentence form (natural language)**â€”"who is doing what, where, and with what emotion"â€”rather than a list of tokens.

3. **Story Composition and Direction**:
Â  Â - **Title Determination**: Devise a "high-sense title" that reflects the theme, conveys the content at a glance, and captures interest.
Â  Â - **Title Logo Placement**:
Â  Â  Â - Create a "title panel" on **Page 1 or Page 2** where the title logo is prominently placed.
Â  Â  Â - **Drawing Instruction**: Include instructions to render the title text itself as "decorative typography" within the image.
Â  Â - **"Setup and Payoff" Structure**:
Â  Â  Â - **Page 1 (The Hook)**: Include a "strong hook (mystery, shock, empathy)" that strongly captures the reader's interest.
Â  Â  Â - **Page 10 (The Punchline)**: The punchline or a cliffhanger leading to the next part.

4. **Rules for Describing Each Page (Strictly Enforced)**:
Â  Â The prompt must always include the following sections.
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **Header**: `High-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full color. Vertical (9:16).`
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **[Character Definition (Fixed)]**:
Â  Â  Â - **Important**: Create a Japanese definition sentence of the **"Character's Appearance Description (clothes, hairstyle, color, accessories)"** analyzed from the initial image, and write it in the **prompt for every page** without changing a single word.
Â  Â  Â - Example Description: "A girl with black bob-cut hair, a red ribbon, golden eyes, wearing a futuristic cyberpunk uniform."
Â  Â 
Â  Â - **[Art Style Definition (Fixed)]**:
Â  Â  Â - **Art Style Analysis and Fixation**: Analyze the input image and define its art style (line thickness, coloring touch, lighting) as a detailed Japanese prompt.
Â  Â  Â - This must also be written in the **prompt for every page**.
Â  Â  Â - Example Description: "Clear, confident main lines, anime coloring with soft gradients, high saturation and vivid colors, dramatic lighting."

Â  Â - **[Panel Layout & Visuals]**:
Â  Â  Â - **Panel Composition**: **Must place 4 to 8 panels** per page. (Fewer than 3 panels is forbidden)
Â  Â  Â - **Eye Guidance**: Specify the placement of each panel (e.g., "top right panel," "bottom left panel") following the Japanese manga format (top right â†’ top left â†’ bottom right â†’ bottom left).
Â  Â  Â - **Content must include the following elements**:
Â  Â  Â  Â 1. **Situation Description**: Character acting, angle, background.
Â  Â  Â  Â 2. **Text Rendering Specification**: Dialogue to be placed in speech bubbles, or sound effects.

Â  Â - **[Page Number]**:
Â  Â  Â - Instruction to draw a small page number (e.g., "1") in the bottom right corner.

## Output Template Example

### Page X

High-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full color. Vertical (9:16).

# [Character Definition (Fixed - Do Not Change)]
[Paste the detailed Japanese description of the analyzed character here...]

# [Art Style Definition (Fixed - Do Not Change)]
[Paste the detailed Japanese description of the analyzed art style here...]

# [Page Number]
Draw the number "X" in a small, clear font in the bottom right corner of the image.

# [Panel Layout & Content (5-8 panels, from top right to bottom left)]

## Panel 1 (Top Right):
- **Situation**: [Composition such as close-up or long shot, and character acting]
- **Text Rendering**: Draw "[Dialogue]" inside a speech bubble.

## Panel 2 (Top Left):
- **Situation**: ...
- **Text Rendering**: Large hand-drawn text "[Onomatopoeia]" in the background. "[Dialogue]" in a speech bubble.

## Panel 3 (Middle Right):
- **Situation**: ...
- **Text Rendering**: ...

(Continue for the number of panels)

## Panel 6 (Bottom Left):
- **Situation**: ...
- **Text Rendering**: ...

Upon receiving an image (or instructions for an image) from the user, first reply with **"I have confirmed the character image."**
Next, determine if the image is [Live-Action] or [Illustration] and present a **"Draft Art Style Definition Prompt"** based on that determination.
2. Story idea proposals (5 total)
```

### No. 81: Comic / Storyboard - High-Altitude Mountaineering Cinematic Collage Prompt

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "scene_description": {
    "subject": "A group of high-altitude mountaineers navigating a treacherous, snow-covered peak during a blizzard.",
    "setting": "High-altitude glacial environment, likely the {argument name="location" default="Himalayas"} or Andes, featuring steep ridgelines, deep crevasses, and sheer ice walls.",
    "atmosphere": "Extreme, hostile, and cinematic. Heavy snowfall, dense white-out fog, and high-velocity wind conditions."
  },
  "visual_elements": {
    "characters": {
      "count": "3 to 4 climbers visible in various frames.",
      "apparel": "Professional heavy-duty red and black down summit suits, yellow high-altitude mountaineering boots (G2/La Sportiva style), climbing harnesses, and oxygen masks with frosted goggles.",
      "equipment": "Technical ice axes, crampons, heavy expedition backpacks, and safety ropes (dynamic climbing line)."
    },
    "actions": {
      "traversing": "Climbers walking along a narrow, snowy knife-edge ridge.",
      "crossing": "Two climbers cautiously walking across a horizontal metal ladder bridged over a deep, dark glacial crevasse.",
      "climbing": "A solo climber using an ice axe to ascend a vertical wall of blue ice.",
      "resting": "Climbers gathered near a small yellow/green flag marker on a snowy plateau."
    },
    "environment_details": {
      "snow_ice": "Texture of wind-swept powder, jagged ice formations, and deep blue glacial rifts.",
      "color_palette": "Dominantly monochromatic white and grey, punctuated by high-visibility {argument name="gear color" default="red"} gear and bright yellow boot accents."
    }
  },
  "technical_specifications": {
    "composition": "Four-panel collage style, wide-angle shots to emphasize the scale of the mountain vs. the humans.",

### No. 82: Product Marketing - Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating high-end, minimalist commercial product photography in the style of luxury brand ads, using an uploaded reference image of the core product as the base.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Using my uploaded reference image as the base, generate a minimalist, high-quality commercial still life photograph with the aesthetic of a luxury brand advertisement.

Preserve the general shape, proportions, and main color scheme of the core product in the reference so that it is instantly recognizable as the same product, but upgrade the overall texture and atmosphere of the image, making it look like an ad for a top-tier international fragrance, skincare item, or high-end electronic product.

Use a vertical 4:5 composition. The background should be a large area of clean, neutral negative space, such as soft off-white, cool gray, or light beige, creating a quiet, restrained, and expensive studio environment. Apart from the core product and a minimal number of necessary supports, do not add any extra decorations. No clutter, no elaborate scene setupâ€”only keep very simple geometric supports (such as a plain white cube, a cylinder, or a thin transparent panel). The supports must be simple and low-profile, existing only to hold and accentuate the product.

Strongly emphasize the material details of the product, and let the lighting fully serve those materials:
Show frosted glass with a fine, soft matte texture, ceramics with a matte or slightly glazed feel, and polished metal with clean, sharp specular highlights. Liquids should have clearly visible viscosity and volume. Avoid any cheap plastic feel, complex patterns, or gaudy stickers; the overall material quality must feel cool, restrained, and luxurious.

Use professional studio lighting: mainly soft, diffused light from softboxes, plus precise rim light outlining the productâ€™s shape. The contours should be crisp and layered, and the shadows should be soft and clean, with no noise or dirty shadow patches. You may use a near-macro viewpoint, moving in closer to the product to highlight materials and details, while preserving ample negative space around the frame so the product can "speak for itself" in the emptiness.

Keep the overall color scheme neutral and calm. The productâ€™s own color can be slightly more saturated, making it the single visual focal point in the scene. Do not use exaggerated gradient backgrounds, flashy colored lighting, or e-commerce promo aesthetics. No large-price text, labels, or cartoon graphics.

The final result must be a high-resolution commercial key visual that looks ready for a magazine back cover or a high-end brand announcement poster: minimalist, quiet, high-end, with the core product confidently centered, surrounded by clean negative space and precisely controlled lighting.
```

### No. 95: E-commerce Main Image - Solarpunk Product Showcase with Bioluminescence

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating a photorealistic solarpunk product showcase. It describes an elegant grid arrangement of sustainable technology products with organic curves, living moss, and bioluminescent glow, set against a verdant living wall background. The scene is lit by golden hour sunlight, aiming for a high-end commercial photography aesthetic that blends Korean minimalist design with natural elements.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A stunning solarpunk product showcase featuring an elegant grid arrangement of sustainable technology products seamlessly integrated with lush botanical elements. The scene displays bio-engineered devices with flowing organic curves and living moss accents arranged in perfect symmetry on a reclaimed wood surface. Each product emanates a soft bioluminescent glow, featuring translucent bio-plastic casings with visible internal plant root systems and flowing water channels. The background reveals a verdant living wall cascade with hanging air-purifying vines, integrated solar panel leaves, and delicate flowering pods that power the displayed technology.

Golden hour sunlight streams through floor-to-ceiling windows, casting warm amber rays that dance across the green foliage and illuminate the products with a dreamy, ethereal backlight. Soft volumetric lighting creates gentle lens flares and highlights the organic textures of both nature and technology. The atmosphere feels optimistic and serene, embodying a harmonious future where innovation and nature coexist beautifully.

Shot from a slightly elevated three-quarter angle using a wide-angle lens with shallow depth of field, creating artistic bokeh in the background vegetation while keeping the product grid in sharp focus. The composition follows rule of thirds with leading lines created by the wooden planks and vine arrangements. Professional commercial photography style with vibrant color grading emphasizing rich emerald greens, warm golden tones, and creamy white highlights. The aesthetic balances minimalist {argument name="design style" default="Korean"} design sensibilities with abundant natural elements, creating an Instagram-worthy visual that suggests premium eco-luxury and sustainable innovation. Photorealistic rendering with high dynamic range, crisp details, and subtle film grain for organic authenticity.
A stylish handwritten signature Willy is elegantly and small letters placed at the Bottom Right corner.
```

### No. 98: E-commerce Main Image - Flat Lay Fashion Editorial Image

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly constrained and detailed prompt for generating a flat lay fashion image suitable for editorial or catalog use. It strictly prohibits depicting any human anatomy and focuses on arranging garments in a geometric, uninhabited composition using specific style and surface parameters.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[OUTFIT_STYLE] = Use the outfit from the reference image | casual utilitarian womenswear | casual mens streetwear
[COMPOSITION_SCHEME] = seated-inspired angular layout | standing-inspired vertical layout | walking-inspired offset layout | dynamic diagonal layout | balance-inspired asymmetric layout | editorial flat-lay grid break | sculptural negative-space layout | yoga-inspired angular balance layout | athletic-inspired directional layout
[SURFACE] = clean matte studio backdrop | soft neutral paper surface | cool tone matte backdrop
[ACCESSORY_MODE] = outfit_integrated | decorative | none

Make a high resolution flat lay fashion image for editorial and catalog use.
Use a strict top down camera angle with a natural 50mm equivalent perspective and perfectly parallel framing.
Set the scene on [SURFACE] with no visible texture seams or edge shadows.

Show only clothing items and approved accessories placed on the surface.
Do not depict or imply any human body, body parts, limbs, skin, joints, or anatomy.
Do not include legs, hips, feet, knees, or any biological structure.

Arrange garments as a flat, uninhabited composition following [COMPOSITION_SCHEME].
Interpret [COMPOSITION_SCHEME] purely as a geometric layout logic, never as a body configuration.
Use angles, spacing, and directional alignment only to suggest balance and posture.

Keep every garment fully flat with zero internal volume.
Force all bottom garments including pants or leggings to remain collapsed, empty, and tension-free.
Do not stretch, contour, wrap, or compress fabric.
Represent bends only through sharp planar folds and angular breaks.
Prohibit smooth curves, rounded forms, seated volume, or body-fit deformation.

Allow folds and wrinkles only as gravity-driven surface creases.
Ensure clothing reads strictly as laid fabric, not worn, inhabited, or shaped by a body.

Select garments and accessories based on {argument name="outfit style" default="OUTFIT_STYLE"}.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is outfit_integrated, include only functionally worn items.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is decorative, allow accessories as independent flat objects.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is none, exclude all accessories entirely.

Use soft diffused daylight from above with gentle shadows directly beneath each item.
Keep spacing balanced with visible negative space around the composition.
Avoid mannequins, models, body silhouettes, stuffing, air filled shapes, extra items, text, logos, or branding.
Ensure clarity, accurate fabric texture, and a calm contemporary aesthetic.
```

Due to strong exaggerated perspective (extreme wide-angle, forced perspective),
the hands and face appear extremely large, being very close to the camera,
and the lower body appears smaller in the back, creating a three-dimensional depth composition.

ğŸŒ Prompt B
Ultra-realistic photo. The moment this character emerges three-dimensionally from a smartphone placed on a table. One hand is reaching towards the viewer, one foot is on the smartphone frame, and the lower body is inside the smartphone. Exaggerated perspective makes the nearby face and hands look large. ### No. 117: Game Asset - Hyper-Realistic Caricature of a Bald Man in a Jersey

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific prompt for generating an 8K, hyper-realistic, stylized caricature figure with extremely exaggerated proportions (large head/torso, short limbs). The subject is bald, glossy-skinned, and wearing a tight white sports jersey, standing on a polished wooden table.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "resolution": "8K ultra high resolution",
  "style": {
    "visual_style": "hyper-realistic, stylized caricature realism",
    "render_quality": "extreme detail, sharp focus on subject, shallow depth of field",
    "lighting_style": "cinematic warm indoor lighting with soft highlights and smooth shadows",
    "color_grading": "warm tones, golden highlights, natural skin tones with glossy reflections"
  },
  "subject": {
    "type": "human-like caricature figure",
    "pose": "standing upright with legs slightly apart",
    "proportions": "extremely exaggerated proportions, very large head and torso, very short limbs",
    "scale": "small, table-height figure",
    "expression": {
      "mouth": "slightly open",
      "eyes": "looking slightly to the side",
      "emotion": "neutral to mildly surprised"
    }
  },
  "head_and_face": {
    "head_shape": "very large, rounded head",
    "hair": "completely bald",
    "skin_texture": "smooth, glossy, reflective with visible moisture",
    "skin_tone": "light to medium skin tone with noticeable red flush on cheeks",
    "facial_features": {
      "cheeks": "very large, swollen appearance with strong redness",
      "chin": "multiple visible folds",
      "eyebrows": "dark, defined eyebrows",
      "eyes": "small relative to head size, natural reflections visible",
      "nose": "small and rounded",
      "lips": "slightly parted, natural color"
    }
  },
  "body": {
    "torso": "extremely large, rounded belly protruding forward",
    "arms": "short and thick arms hanging down",
    "hands": "small hands with short fingers",
    "legs": "short, thick legs",
    "feet": "bare feet, small toes visible",
    "skin_detail": "glossy surface with visible highlights, subtle texture, reflective sheen"
  },
  "clothing": {
    "top": {
      "type": "short-sleeve sports jersey",
      "color": "{argument name="jersey color" default="white"}",
      "fit": "very tight, stretched over torso",
      "logos": [
        {
          "placement": "center chest",
          "description": "sports brand logo in blue"
        },
        {
          "placement": "left chest",
          "description": "gold shield-shaped emblem"
        },
        {
          "placement": "right chest",
          "description": "circular crest with crown and letters"
        }
      ],
      "details": "blue accent stripes on shoulders"
    },
    "bottom": "no visible pants or shorts"
  },
  "environment": {
    "setting": "indoor room",
    "surface": {
      "type": "wooden table",
      "texture": "polished wood grain with reflections"
    },
    "background": {
      "focus": "heavily blurred",
      "elements": [
        "warm glowing lights",
        "candle-like light sources",
        "dark interior shapes"
      ],
      "bokeh": "large circular light bokeh"
    }
  },
  "props": {
    "left_side": {
      "object": "transparent glass"
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
